<H>{@sāraḷā mahābhārata
<>udyoga paba
<>gaṇeśaṅka bandanā@}
<P>jaẏatu dadhibāmana prasanne rudra debatā
<P>maṅgaḷa bighnarāja bhūta bhabiṣya gyāṁtā | 1 |
<P>maṅgaḷa sadānanda deba lambodara
<P>sapata sindhu gopyagalā yāhāra udara | 2 |
<P>maṅgaḷa paramabrahma sarūpa bīṇāẏeka
<P>pāśa aṁkuśa gajabadana aṭa triẏambaka | 3 |
<P>meru tattulya yāhāra kiñchita beniākhi
<P>abaniḷe chāhiṁle tu ye koṭi brahmāṇḍa dekhi | 4 |
<P>ḍibi ḍibi bajāi yāhāra ḍāki ḍambharu
<P>hr̥de paitā yāhāra ananta nāga pheru | 5 |
<P>svāmī tripura badhagalā yāhāra buddhi baḷe
<P>binaẏe anubrate nātha muṁ tumbhara pādataḷe | 6 |
<P>lāṅgaṭa bhrūṅgaṭa ye bikaṭa batranāṭe
<P>mahābharaha tāṇḍaba āropaṇa saṁkoṭe | 7 |
<P>śrī bighnarāja śrīcaraṇa kamaḷe
<P>mama citta bhaji ho tahiṁ rahu ye bhrasaḷe | 8 |
[MBO-06-2]
<P>byāsaṁkara srijane deba prasanna bighnarāja
<P>karaṇa hoi lekhana kaluṭi aiśuryya | 9 |
<P>ẏe saṁsāra madhye muhiṁ se dekhili sarūpa
<P>tuhi se harantā deba kaḷikāḷa darpa | 10 |
<P>kaḷiyuga bañchantā nātha prasanne paramayogī
<P>dinakara bibādeṇa tu kāḷadarpa bhāñji | 11 |
<P>sadaẏe nārāẏaṇa tu prasanne rudrakāśī
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷa dāsa talaẏe abhyāsi | 12 |
<H>{@pāṇḍabaṅka indraprasthe prabeśa, dhr̥tarāṣṭra sañjaẏa saṁbāda
<>o dhaumya purohitaṅkara dūtapaṇe
<>hastinā gamana@}
<P>śuṇa ho caitana śrī mahābhāratha udiyoga paboṅg kathā
<P>yāhā hetu karipārile sabhāẏe hoiba bakatā | 1 |
<P>yebaṇa grantha śuṇile adhārmikahiṁ hoẏe bhigyaṁ
<P>yāha śuṇileṭi prāṇī huanti sarbagyaṁ | 2 |
<P>udiyoga paboṅg kathā hr̥dagate laẏe kale
<P>śāhāsraku jitā hoi ẏehā unyeṣi pārile | 3 |
<P>udiyoga paṛhile dr̥śa hoai buddhi
<P>udiyoga paṛhile prāpata hoai ruddhi siddhi | 4 |
<P>udiyoga boliṇa yebaṇa grantha paboṅg
<P>dharma artha kāma mokṣa prāpata ẏethuṁ sarba | 5 |
<P>caubarga sampada ye prāpata brahmagyāna
<P>āṣya dhana santāna hoiba barddhamāna | 6 |
<P>yāhā se srijanā kaleka agasti
<P>muhiṁ tāhā bañchāili bicitra śuddha pothi | 7 |
[MBO-06-3]
<P>udiyoga paboṅg śunimā nare bāṇī
<P>subuddhi paṇḍita sugyaṁ hoiba ẏehā śuṇi | 8 |
<P>baibasuta manu pucchākale agasti
<P>ẏethu anantare hoilā yisa rīti | 9 |
<P>śubhayoge pāṇḍabe bāhāra matsyadeśuṁ
<P>ākāśe maṅgaḷa dhuni śubhai pāṇḍabaṁkara āsuṁ | 10 |
<P>birāṭa āgiāṇi samadaṇḍa gheni
<P>pacheṇa pañchāḷa kumāranta gheni śrīkhaṇḍī bhrātha beni | 11 |
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇā dropatī ye koḷa sambhāṣaṇe
<P>pāñchāḷīki prabodhile bahuta sanamāne | 12 |
<P>gopāḷī nadīkūḷe birāṭa prabodhi
<P>aneka binoẏī hoile birāṭa yathābidhi | 13 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe ye prabodhi bacana prakāśi
<P>bāhuḍa birāṭa tu parama kalyāṇa hoasi | 14 |
<P>birāṭa praṇapatya ye yujheṣṭhiṁka padmapāẏe
<P>muhiṁ yāiṁ kinā svāmī indrapraśasta yāẏe | 15 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile ho daṇḍa ghenigale
<P>mānagobinda kopa karibanā parathāṭha dekhile | 16 |
<P>sahodraṁka nimante kāḷaka bulili ghora bane
<P>ābara kimpe dharma laṁghibi aḷapa ye dine | 17 |
<P>śānti samārjane āmbhe na karibā kaḷi
<P>aṣṭa abadhāne ye śatr̥ku sambhāḷi | 18 |
<P>birāṭa śrīkhaṇḍi ye bāhuḍile sanya gheni
<P>tahuṁ se pāṇḍabe caḷile dibasa rajanī | 19 |
<P>pañchatiriśa dibase prabeśa indrapraśaste
<P>nagra bhitare yāi rahile pañchu bhrāthe | 20 |
<P1>12|2–śānti bhaji rahibā bahuta sanamāne | (ja, da, ṇa, ka, ba)
<P1>18|2–aṣṭa abadhāne śatr̥ku saṁghāri | (ṭa, gha)
[MBO-06-4]
<P>bhāmasena boilā deba yibānā āstānaku
<P>dekhibā nāhi ki driyothana dhuśāsana bhīṣma droṇa karṇṇaṁku | 21 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile jāṇimā tadanta
<P>bāratā pāi mānagobinda niai kinā āmbhanta | 22 |
<P>bijaẏe mānagobinda sambharba āstāne
<P>bāratā jaṇāile yāiṁ deśāuramāne | 23 |
<P>svāmī pāṇḍaba āgata boli jaṇāile haraṣe
<P>indrapraśasta rājye āsi hoile parabeśe | 24 |
<P>chāragaṇa mukhuṁ ẏesanaka bākya śuṇi
<P>śakuni pratibākya diai hāde puṇi | 25 |
<P>pāṇḍabe yebe prabeśa hoile indrapraśaste
<P>ratha gaja aśva pādānti achanti saṅge kete | 26 |
<P>ḍagara patibākya deba sābadhāna bhabatu
<P>birāṭa daṇḍa gheni bāhuḍi galā dharmapathuṁ | 27 |
<P>pāṇḍaba pāñchajaṇa kumāra abhimanyu
<P>pāñchāḷa kumāra tule bāḷuta ye tanu | 28 |
<P>dropatī subhadrā ye ābara uttarabāḷī
<P>ẏeteka tule dekhilu āna nāhiṁ aguḷi | 29 |
<P>sañjaẏe kahile dhr̥tarāṣṭaṁka āgare
<P>pāṇḍabe prabeśa hoile indrapraśasta nabare | 30 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa boile ho karibā kemanta
<P>bho daiba puruṣa mote hoibā upagata | 31 |
<P>driyodhana kaṇṭhe bijekaru kinā sarasvatī
<P>pāṇḍabe kaurabe yehne hoanti pīrati | 32 |
<P>sañjaẏe boile rājā na kara biḷāpa
<P>dharma abaśeṣe āsi barddhuta hoilā ki prāpa | 33 |
[MBO-06-5]
<P>yujheṣṭhi hr̥dagate nāhiṁnā anīti
<P>sarbe manda aṭanti nā tohora santati | 34 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi hr̥dagate yebe bhābiba anīti
<P>ābara kuru pāṇḍabe kāhiṁ loḍu pīrati | 35 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa bolanti śuṇa ho sañjaẏe
<P>manukāḷa bañchāile baśiṣṭhaṁka śatapoẏe | 36 |
<P>biśvābasu gandharba ye pūrbe basithile svarge
<P>bhmabigata hoile se dr̥bhāsāṁka rāge | 37 |
<P>mahītaḷe rājya se kaleka ẏekamanu
<P>kāḷe utapatti hoile śate aṣṭauttara tanu | 38 |
<P>gata śāpya pāiṁ se dr̥bhāsāṁku tapakale
<P>pitākaiṁ gheniṇa se svargare basile | 39 |
<P>bho sañjaẏe ẏesaneka pātaka kalai muhiṁ kāhuṁ
<P>anamite kopakali bidura paramārtha kahuṁ kahuṁ | 40 |
<P>sādhu sādhu bidura ho tohora jībati
<P>boilu kuṭumba barddhute tote śoka apramiti | 41 |
<P>śuṇiṇa kope muṁ tote prahāra kalaiṁ pāde
<P>ẏeḍe baḍa baṁśa mora buḍilā mānagobinda parasāde | 42 |
<P>sañjaẏe boilā rāẏe bistāra na karani ẏehu kathā
<P>apāda cintile maṅgaḷa nohai sarbastā | 43 |
<P>āpaṇe yāhā arji tāhā karma boli
<P>anīti saṁsāre ẏehā pratakṣe dekhili | 44 |
<P>āho baibasuta manu pāṇḍabe bije kariachanti indraraśaste
<P>lakṣe dvija gheniṇa bije dhaumya purohite | 45 |
<P>dharmara nandana ye mahāguru dekhi
<P>uṭhile pāṇḍabe begeṁ āstāna upekṣi | 46 |
<P1>36|2–manukāḷa bañchāile paṇḍuṁkara poẏe |(ṭa, jha)
[MBO-06-6]
<P>pādāarghya deiṇa ye caraṇe kale dibyapūjā
<P>samasta kuśaḷa ye pucchanti dharmarājā | 47 |
<P>kanaka uturī paitā dileka nei kandhe
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile durgati bañchilu tohora prasāde | 48 |
<P>kanaka āsana dileka dharmarāẏe
<P>samasta kuśaḷa pachāranti dhaumya ye paṇḍāẏe | 49 |
<P>dhaumya purohite boile puchuṁ āmbhe tuku
<P>bhāinta gheni yibunā hastinā sabhāku | 50 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile ẏe kathā na miḷai yugate
<P>muhiṁ aneka durgati bañchili banaste | 51 |
<P>se mohora sodara kariba mote cintā
<P>bāratā pāi mānagobinda yebe āmbhanta niantā | 52 |
<P>tebe se jāṇanti nā tāhāra nikaḷaṁkara hiẏā
<P>pāpa buddhi āchāraṇa kalāka kurunāhā | 53 |
<P>apoṣaka sodara abhagata bāḷa
<P>anāchārī bhāriyā pāpaṣaẏa kāḷa | 54 |
<P>abhabī maitra kaḷahakārī sūpakāra
<P>bibādī bairi bhūmi asahara | 55 |
<P>kāḷarudra debata tīrtha asurabhogī
<P>paṇḍita loke ẏehā dūrahuṁ parityāgi | 56 |
<P>purohite boile paṇḍa dhr̥tarāṣṭa
<P>ẏeka pitāuṁ janama sodara tumbhe beni aṭa | 57 |
<P>nīra kṣīra yehne hoai ye abheda
<P>parameṣi pārile ẏehā hoi nā paramāda | 58 |
<P>biśeṣe kaniṣṭha se ābara baẏase mattagarba
<P>tāhāra yeteka doṣa upekṣā karibāka sarba | 59 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile tāta se sahodra poḍu poḍu
<P>bhmañjāi basāi bhīmāku khuāile biṣalaḍu | 60 |
[MBO-06-7]
<P>bhojana śeṣe biṣa ghārilā yetebeḷe
<P>rātrakāḷe bānddhakari melile agāda jaḷe | 61 |
<P>jadura ghare bhiāile bāruṇābante kūṭe
<P>jau sajaḷasa guāghata ābara chaṇapaṭe | 62 |
<P>niśākāḷe puṇa se dileka gharapoḍi
<P>dharmara baḷe sinā galu tahuṁ ye uburi | 63 |
<P>puṇi kapaṭa pāśāẏe bhiāile mahāmantrī śakuni
<P>kūṭa upāẏe kari se mohora samasta rājyabhāra gheni | 65 |
<P>āpaṇe āstāne basi āmbhanta basāilā sabhātaḷe
<P>dhuśāsana dhariacchi dropatīra bāḷe | 65 |
<P>ābara dhariṇa bibasana kale satī
<P>dharmara baḷe se uburilā dropatī | 66 |
<P>ghoṣayātrā kāḷe se kaimeka nāme bane
<P>atihiṁ jhiṁghāsa sahi nuārile debagaṇe | 67 |
<P>citrasena gandharba driyodhanaku bānddhanelā rāge
<P>se gandharbaku jiṇilā arjuna raṇaraṅge | 68 |
<P>pañchāḷa kaṭake yāiṁ kaleka yebaṇahiṁ kathā
<P>tumbhe ki pāi achanā tahiṁra bāratā | 69 |
<P>banastuṁ dropatīṁki hari heuthilā beḷe
<P>keteheṁ durāpada ye sahibā sarbakāḷe | 70 |
<P>bipatti paḍai se dharmakathā kahuṁ kahuṁ
<P>beda śāhāsra ābara sata houacchi kāhuṁ | 71 |
<P>rājakuḷe jāta hoi mohora ẏeheneka abastā
<P>kuru pāṇḍabe pīrati āu nohiba sarbastā | 72 |
<P>āditya debatā yebe pacchime hoi ude
<P>pūrbe asta yebe nohibe abade | 73 |
<P>candra naṣṭa yebe hoibe paurṇṇamī
<P>jaḷa praḷaẏa yebe naśiba sarbabhūmi | 74 |
[MBO-06-8]
<P>dhātubāda purusa yebe na karibeka br̥ṣṭi
<P>parbata upare yebe naḷinīdaḷa puṭi | 75 |
<P>jaḷa bhitare yebe upuciāiba śiḷa
<P>sola bheḷā yebe buḍibāka jaḷa | 76 |
<P>stirī hoiba puruṣa, dibasa hoiba rāti
<P>jaḷa yebe tapata hoiba śītaḷa hoiba bahati | 77 |
<P>āho prohite haṭakarma purāṇe ẏehā aṣṭābatra muni kahi
<P>ẏete bāge hoile yujheṣṭhi deba ẏehā ki sahai | 78 |
<P>mohora beḷe yebe ẏehā muṁ sahi pārai
<P>nirañjana debatā thaḷare biṣa muṁ bharai | 79 |
<P>śibadroha karai alaṁghita niẏama
<P>nicaẏe saṁkalpa mohora hoilā sāṁgrāma | 80 |
<P>purohite boile kāḷabhraṣṭa hoilā
<P>sahadebe boile prohite kaḷi prabarttilā | 81 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile śuṇimā prohite
<P>hastinā yiba tumbhe āmbhara nimante | 82 |
<P>sampada mora māḍi basilā kurupati
<P>abichāra puruṣe mote karāile aprīti | 83 |
<P>dhr̥tirāṣṭa agrate kahiba tumbhe yāiṁ
<P>indrapraśasta rājya khaṇḍi mote deu kurusāiṁ | 84 |
<P>tumbhe ta purohite mora baṁśara parama guru
<P>maṇāiṁ kahiba mote dhr̥tarāṣṭa daẏākaru | 85 |
<P>purohite boile āmbhe yibuṁ tohora bole
<P>kisa uttara karibuṁ āmbhe mānagobinda nāstikale | 86 |

<P1>78 prohite śāsra purāṇa yebe anyo anye hoi
<>tebe ẏe kathā hoiba kahi nuārai | ka, da
[MBO-06-9]
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile tumbhe karibaṭi kisa
<P>se nāsti boile tumbhe bāhuḍiṇa āsa | 87 |
<P>bijekarṇṇakuṇḍaḷa meruśūḷa dilā muku
<P>ẏe apūrba padārtha nei dia dhr̥tarāṣṭaṁku | 88 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debaṁka nirādhāra bākya śuṇi
<P>caḷike purohite ye dūtakāra jāṇi | 89 |
<P>tuleṇa ghenile tāṁkara lakṣeka bāḷaśiṣi
<P>hastinā rājye purohite prabeśa hoile āsi | 90 |
<P>driyodhana bije karicchi yama ye praśaste
<P>karṇṇa śaṁkuni dhuśāsana śalya ye sahite | 91 |
<P>purohite prabeśa yāiṁ hoile sannidhāne
<P>dūruṁ dekhi śaṁkuni kahilā bidyamāne | 92 |
<P>boilā dhaumya purohite āsuchanti yahiṁki
<P>ke kemanta ẏehā ye bichārani dekhi | 93 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā tu se paṇḍita mahāgyāṁtā
<P>śūrabanta puruṣa tu bhūta bhabiṣya jāṇantā | 94 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā tu se mantrī cūḍāmaṇi
<P>mānagobinde tu sampada bhogya karāilu āṇi | 95 |
<P>pāṇḍabaṁka darpa marddilu tohora buddhibaḷe
<P>pañchurājya bhogya karāilu kutūhoḷe | 96 |
<P>āho agocara gocara tu bhabiṣyata gyāṁtā
<P>adr̥śya dr̥śyahiṁ se kathā bichārantā | 97 |
<P>śaṁkuni boilā tu bujha upanesi
<P>dūtakāra paṇe ẏehānta yujheṣṭhi dile peṣi | 98 |
<P>ẏehikathā pramāṇa hoibanā yugate
<P>ẏe puṇa āsiachanti grāma māgibā nimante | 99 |
<P>ẏesanaka kahilā śaṁkuni bhūta bhabiṣya sandeśa
<P>dhaumya purohita āsi ye hoile prabeśa | 100 |
[MBO-06-10]
<P>āsana samārjana ye kalāka kururāẏe
<P>ati ānande praḷamba sakaḷa sandehe | 101 |
<P>kuśaḷa bāratā ye pucchākale dhaumye
<P>ārogya nirāpada hoi bratiachanā sarbakṣame | 102 |
<P>samsta kuśaḷa boli ye boile kaurabe
<P>tubhe ẏebe gabana kala keuṁṇa parastābe | 103 |
<P>dhaumya purohite boile tumbhe śuṇimā dhārmika dhr̥tirāṣṭi
<P>banabāsa dr̥rgatiru pārahoi ẏebe aile yujheṣṭhi | 104 |
<P>āho bāhāra nagrare āsi rahichanti indra ye praśaste
<P>tohora tāhānta śaṁkhoḷibā yogāi yugate | 105 |
<P>bābu tohora rājya deśa nohai ki indra ye praśasta
<P>nagra bhramaṇi karigale pāṇḍabe hoibe uṣata | 106 |
<P>bābu amr̥ta biṣa thāiṭi ẏehi jibhyā
<P>sadabuddhi thāuṁ thāuṁ asadabuddhi kemante debā | 107 |
<P>bābu dharme āśre karithile ho mānagobinda
<P>kadācitte praṇīṁkiṭi na paḍai pramāda | 108 |
<P>bābu sahodra sambhāḷile bahuta hoai dharma
<P>samasta kāḷaku kathā thāiṭi satyadharma | 109 |
<P>uṭha bābu indrapraśastaku bege yibā
<P>gauroba kari pāṇḍabanta gheniṇa āsibā | 110 |
<P>bābu kuḷare putreka upujile baṁśa karaiṭi rakṣā
<P>ihaloke paraloke pūrai manabāñcchā | 111 |
<P>bābu boila ye tumbhe āmbhara parama guru
<P>dharmaku prāpata hoibu nā tu yebe antara na dharu | 112 |
<P>driyodhana boilā paṇḍāẏe raha raha
<P>pāilu prastāba tumbhe kicchihiṁ na kaha | 113 |
[MBO-06-11]
<P>tumbhanta piṣilā se yahiṁra nimante
<P>tāhā niryyāpa kari kimpe na kahaṭi mote | 114 |
<P>purohite boile tumbhe sarbaguṇa lakṣaṇa
<P>paramana jāṇanta tumbhe ati bicakṣaṇa | 115 |
<P>yebe tāhānta tu nagalu pāgchoṭi
<P>āpaṇā karmaku santāpilā se yujheṣṭhi | 116 |
<P>apāra purasari boilā āmbhaṁku
<P>indrapraśasta paḍākhiṇḍi deba ki tāhāṁku | 117 |
<P>ẏeka paḍāke se thāntu sakaḷa prāṇī
<P>driyodhanara mukuṭa kampilā tāhā śuṇi | 118 |
<P>āho purohite tumbhe kuḷara brāhmaṇa
<P>ẏesana bākya kahibā tumbhara kebaṇa kāraṇa | 119 |
<P>ẏesaneka tama basilā mora bakṣasthaḷe
<P>āna hoile ki prāṇa thāāntā ẏetebeḷe | 120 |
<P>tumbhe ye purohite dekhibā arthe gala
<P>ohokuḷa artha tumbhe manāsibānā bhala | 121 |
<P>purohite boile bābu ẏe se bhala bichāra
<P>śūrabanta guṇabanta jībana tohroa sāra | 122 |
<P>beni sodare tumbhe āmbhara bola kale
<P>baṁśa udita hoiba dina yiba bhale | 123 |
<P>mānagobinda boilā mahataṁkara bākya
<P>samasyāẏe jāṇiluni ẏesaneka bibeka | 124 |
<P>ẏeka paḍā khaṇḍiẏe pāile yujheṣṭhi
<P>sakaḷa kathā kuśaḷa hontā purantā manatuṣṭi | 125 |
<P>bhīṣma droṇa bhūriśrabā samakacche
<P>āmbhara śubhabākya sumaribānā pache | 126 |
<P>ẏete boli purohite ohlāile āstānu
<P>nāsikāẏe hātha dei hasanti kurutanu | 127 |
[MBO-06-12]
<P>lajjābhara hoiṇa se caḷile purohite
<P>yāiṇa prabeśa hoile indra ye praśaste | 128 |
<P>manare birasa ye haraṣabhāba tāṁka nāhiṁ
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe jāṇile hr̥dareṇa lāi | 129 |
<P>manara birasa dekhi pachāranti mahārāje
<P>subidhāne prasannagata na diśi mohora kāryye | 130 |
<P>manara birase se badanti deba dhaumye
<P>yehne prāpata hoẏe ye yāhāra karme | 131 |
<P>dvandeṇa baṛhilā ho yāhāra prakr̥ti
<P>sadā gacchai ki tāhāra mana śānti | 132 |
<P>samasta sañchapi ye kahanti deba dhaumye
<P>kauroba pāṇḍabaṁka kathā nuhai nā sāmye | 133 |
<P>dvandaku icchā yebe tohora hāde acchi
<P>aṣṭāṅgamate āra nohoinā kicchi | 134 |
<P>āho tu yebe sahibu bābu tebe se rahai tora baṁśa
<P>tohora na sahile ohokuḷa yiba nāśa | 135 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi deba boile ye mora ẏekādaśa baraṣa
<P>paṇḍu mahārāẏe ye hoile prāṇe nāśa | 136 |
<P>uṇeiśa baraṣa mote ruhāile jatughare
<P>tahuṁṇa uburilu pañchabiṁśa baraṣare | 137 |
<P>pañchabiṁśa baraṣare hoilu banabāṣī
<P>pāñchāḷīku labhilu mahalākha nāśi | 138 |
<P>tahiṁra uttāre ye ailu rājyaku
<P>puṇi paśita na dile āmbhaṁku hastinā bhmabanaku | 139 |
<P>samaẏeka rahiluṁ āmbhe bāruṇābanta nagrare
<P>kapāṭapāśā bhiāile ghenile rājyabhāre | 140 |
[MBO-06-13]
<P>puṇihiṁ dvādaśa baraṣa bulilu ghorabane
<P>baraṣe teradina ye rahilu gopyāne | 141 |
<P>āho purohite keteheṁ dukha sahibu sabhābe
<P>pañchastorī baraṣa hoilāni baẏasa mote ẏebe | 142 |
<P>rājāra kuḷe āmbhe hoilu jāẏe
<P>anartha diśuacchi garu mahābhaẏe | 143 |
<P>tumbhe mote sākṣī hoithibāka deba dhaumye
<P>nicaẏa brata mora hoilā sāṁgrāme | 144 |
<P>ẏesanaka bākya kahante dharmarāẏe
<P>meru ohāḍe sūryya kāḷa hoẏe | 145 |
<P>sandhyākaiṁ bijaẏe kaleka debadharme
<P>ye yāhāra anarūpe paśile nijakarme | 146 | || 158 ||
<H>{@yudhiṣṭhiraṅka samara pratijñā–dhr̥tarāṣṭa, bhūrisarba,
<>dhaumya o biduraṅkara duryyodhanaku
<>pañchapaḍā prārthanā ebaṁ biduraṅku
<>yudhiṣṭhiraṅka nikaṭaku preraṇa@}
<P>raẏaṇī prabhāte ye bijaẏe kurupati
<P>bidurakaiṁ hakārile dhr̥tarāṣṭa mahākṣatrī | 1 |
<P>āho bidura tumbhe yāani yujheṣṭhiṁka kati
<P>dharmakaim āśrekari thāāntu sehu brati | 2 |
<P>āho paṇḍita hoi se anarthī hoile
<P>pr̥thī na thibanā tāhāra na sahile | 3 |
<P>āho driyodhana aneka jhiṁghāsilā tāhāṁku
<P>se doṣamāna hāde debaṭi jāṇa muku | 4 |
<P1>145|2–anartha se diśuacchi mote arthalābha prāẏe |(jha, ka)
[MBO-06-14]
<P>āho duṣṭaṁkara mattagarba śānti hoibā yāẏe
<P>tetekāḷa pariyante sahi rahithāu samaẏe | 5 |
<P>aneka prabodhiṇa ye kahile tiāriṇa
<P>ohokuḷa baṁśa sa kariba rakṣaṇa | 6 |
<P>pitāra bacane se bidura mahātamā
<P>caḷai indrapraśaste se bhārathakuḷa brahmā | 7 |
<P>udaẏe dinakara ye beḷa pāñchaghaḍi
<P>bidura bheṭile ye kāḷabeḷa uttāri | 8 |
<P>ẏe bidhi pūjā ye binaẏe debarāẏe
<P>sabhāre basile se ambubatīra tanaẏe | 9 |
<P>bhīma arjuna nakuḷa sahadeba mānya gheni
<P>ẏemānanta gheni kuśaḷa bāratā pachānti anyoanyi | 10 |
<P>banasta bāratā ye bidure parakāśi
<P>yujheṣṭhi deba sarba kahile sambhāṣi | 11 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile tāta banaste baḍa sukha
<P>ẏe se bichāre pāuchuṁ baḍa dukha | 12 |
<P>bidure boile yebe banaste baḍa sustha tote
<P>sodara jhiṁghāsi tu ailu ki nimante | 13 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile muṁ ye hoili banabāsī
<P>tahiṁki kaurobe bmote yāānti jhiṁghāsi | 14 |
<P>bidure boile bābu mahata janaṁku
<P>dharmeṇa kaṣaṇa paḍai kahai muhiṁ tuku | 15 |
<P>bābu tu ye mahata paṇḍita dhārmika kuḷaśīḷa
<P>sugyānī puruṣa tu ye sahibu sakaḷa | 16 |
<P>puṇa samaẏeka sahuki na dharma
<P>samaẏeke duṣṭanta paḍai asama | 17 |
[MBO-06-15]
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile tāta ẏemanta na kaha
<P>yemante kuru pāṇḍabe baṛhai sandeha | 18 |
<P>tumbhe paṇḍita ye mahābhigyaṁ subuddhi
<P>tumbhe thāi benipakṣa karibanā sanddha | 19 |
<P>to tahuṁ pitāmaha nāhiṁta hitakārī
<P>mama bākya gheni yāa hastinā nagarī | 20 |
<P>sampada māḍi basiacchi mānacatrabratī
<P>abichāra kari mote karāile abhyārthī | 21 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile tāta dhr̥tarāṣṭaku kaha
<P>śānti bhajiṇa kathā yemanta hoiba raha | 22 |
<P>indrapraśasta rājya pañchabiṁśa sahasra yojana māḍi
<P>yamapraśasta aṣṭādaśa sahasra yojana sthaḷī aguḷī | 23 |
<P>jaintā kaṭaka dui ahibrata dui sahasra yojana aguḷi
<P>koḍiẏe sahasra yojana bāruṇābanta sthaḷī | 24 |
<P>hastinā kaṭaka pandara sahasra yojana ye deśa
<P>ẏenyāẏuṁ pañcharājya lakṣe yojana ye pakāśa | 25 |
<P>sukheṇa bhoga karai pañchu rājya māḍi
<P>kiñchita kari deu mote paḍā pāñchakhaṇḍi chāḍi | 26 |
<P>bhāinta gheniṇa thāikinā kaṇake
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa caraṇe khaṭithibi dr̥ṛha bākye | 27 |
<P>athabā paḍā pāñchakhaṇḍi yebe na diai muku
<P>abaśya saṁgrāma hoiba kahili dr̥ṛhabākya tuku | 28 |
<P>muṁ yebe tāhāra tule samara na karai
<P>bho pitā bidura tumbhara muṁ pādapadme hārai | 29 |
<P1>22|2 paḍā pāñchakhaṇḍi āmbhanta yemanta diāa |(ba, ka)
<P1>22|2–śānti hoi yemante prīti hoi raha |(pha, ña)
<P1>29|2–bho pitā tohora caraṇe droha muṁ karai |(cha, da, ba, pha)
[MBO-06-16]
<P>dharma dharma sumari tahuṁ ye caḷile pitāmaha
<P>aniryyāpa kathā mote lāgilā sandeha | 30 |
<P>caḷile bidura se nirādhāra bacana śuṇi
<P>yujheṣṭhi debaṁku tiāranti leuṭi puṇapuṇi | 31 |
<P>bābu samarakaiṁ tu yebe kalu icchā
<P>pratakṣe jāṇunā bhīṣma droṇaṁkara kaicchā | 32 |
<P>idaṁ pratibākya ye badaẏanti mahātamā
<P>icchāmr̥ta gāṅgeba pratakṣe jāṇu sinā | 33 |
<P>bābu tumbhaṁku hāranti sinā uprodha kari yuddhe
<P>sarūpa saṁgrāme ke tāhānta jiṇima raṇamadhye | 34 |
<P>jāṇunā droṇe ye pāṭharuṣi gotrī
<P>nimiṣake mahībhārā kari pārai nibr̥tti | 35 |
<P>hāthare śahasra thile nāhiṁ tāhāṁku mr̥tu
<P>kāḷa bebhāre se jāṇai brahmatattu | 36 |
<P>kr̥paāchāryya ye bhārata kuḷa brahmā
<P>kaḷapī aẏuṣa yoddhā se aṭai aśastamā | 37 |
<P>mādrīra sodara se śalya mahārathī
<P>nārāẏaṇa śaṁkita yāhāra samara dekhi | 38 |
<P>bhūriśrabā bālmīka ābara jadyaratha somadatta
<P>ajaẏe raṇayoddhā se atulya durānta | 39 |
<P>karṇṇa mahāmalla ye tohora sohodra aṭai
<P>kehi na bratai ye tāhāku samare bheṭai | 40 |
<P>abhedakapaca bajra chaurī amr̥ta kuṇḍaḷa chāpante karṇṇe
<P>ke tāhāku samāna hoiba ẏe tini bhmabane | 41 |
<P>bajra paśupatra bighāta na bhedai yāhāra gātre
<P>jharai amr̥ta rasa yāhāra benikarṇṇa pātre | 42 |
<P>ẏe mahī maṇḍaḷe paḍai yāhāra kathā
<P>tāhākaiṁ jiṇimāku tu ki sāmarathā | 43 |
[MBO-06-17]
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile tāta tu na kahani ẏehā
<P>anāsta lokanta kāḷe dharmahiṁ se sāhā | 44 |
<P>sarbathā prāṇīnta yebe chāḍibāka dharma
<P>dhātubāda puruṣa kimpā tāhā karānti janama | 45 |
<P>bho tāta baḷabīryya thāuṁ thāuṁ yebe hīnabīryya hoilā
<P>sañjaẏe jāṇimā se prāṇī jīuṁ jīuṁ malā | 46 |
<P>tāhānta jiṇimāku muṁ sāmaratha nohile
<P>bibādaku icchā ki hoiba mohora beḷe | 47 |
<P>caḷa caḷa pitāmaha na bolani mote ẏehā
<P>anāsta lokaku se dharama hoi sāhā | 48 |
<P>tuḷa śukḷa pañchamī puṇi uttama bāra
<P>mūḷā nakṣatraku ye bhogathilā se dinara | 49 |
<P>baba nāme karaṇa dhr̥ti nāme yoga
<P>caḷanti bidura tahuṁ hastināku bega | 50 |
<P>idaṁ bākye samāpata paboṅg udiyoge
<P>bidura prabeśa hoile dhr̥tarāṣṭaṁkara āge | 51 |
<P>muṇohi uttāre bāhāra mandire bijaẏe
<P>ẏekasthāne basile dhatarāṣṭa sañjaẏe | 52 |
<P>sañjaẏe boile abadhāna debasvāmī
<P>bidure bijaẏe tāta chāmure paraṇāmi | 53 |
<P>idaṁ bākya dhr̥tirāṣṭa bidura sampāda
<P>sarba kuśaḷa sodara mahā paribandha | 54 |
<P>bidure boile deba kuśaḷe yebe cintā
<P>pāṇḍabaṁkara kāryya kimpe na karasi sanddhagatā | 55 |
<P>apāra kaṣṭe se ye bane gale sebi
<P>nandana sahodra tora kesaneke na bhābi | 56 |
<P>dhr̥tirāṣṭe boile bābu bheṭile ki yujheṣṭhi
<P>mama putra hite se bane hele kaṣṭa | 57 |
[MBO-06-18]
<P>bāḷuta kāḷahuṁ se hoile parama yogī
<P>sarbadā kāḷe se dharmaku na laṁghi | 58 |
<P>bābu pāpakaiṁ bhaẏe se karai sarbakāḷe
<P>dharmaku āśrekari bratanti ẏetebeḷe | 59 |
<P>bidure boile deba kahilu tu dharma
<P>tohora putragoṭi se kebaṇa lakṣaṇe janma | 60 |
<P>na thāuṁ thāuṁ prāṇī hoai mandāchārī
<P>ketekāḷa paryyante tāku dharma thiba ābori | 61 |
<P>tuhi ye se mabaṁśe bihantā bidhātā
<P>tu se chāḍilunā sehi putraṁkara cintā | 62 |
<P>bidure boile yujheṣṭhi bānapraśaste
<P>pūrbanyāẏuṁ kari se sama dai tote | 63 |
<P>mukuiṁ basāi se aneka kahilā pīrati
<P>paḍā pāñchakhaṇḍi se māgai abhyathī | 64 |
<P>ẏeteka pāile se rahiba mana mr̥cchi
<P>śānti bhaji rahiba dvanda ne hibāka kicchi | 65 |
<P>tu ye parama guru hastinā pañchu svarge
<P>tohora thāuṁ kuṭumbe se anyoanyi kebaṇa bāge | 66 |
<P>bho tāta yābata dharma tābata karma gacchi
<P>aniryyāpta nirodhi ẏebe ohokuḷa rakṣī | 67 |
<P>āho tuta amārga adr̥śya benicachu
<P>tu abā kāhāku svāmī ḍapodha kama achu | 68 |
<P>bho tāta putranta bhañjāi ẏebe kahimela kathā
<P>mattagarba doṣeṇa pramāda paḍai sarbathā | 69 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa boile bābu tu aṭu he sarbagyaṁ
<P>dhārmika bibeka paṇḍita tu aṭu mahābhigyaṁ | 70 |
[MBO-06-19]
<P>putranta tiāra bābu yemanta hoẏe prīti
<P>ohokuḷa abibāde bābu hoiba sadagati | 71 |
<P>bhūrisarbanta hakārāi andha kauroba
<P>ẏekānte basāi kahai priẏabhāba | 72 |
<P>bho tāta somabaṁśara dhāraṇa tu aṭu adhikārī
<P>kauroba baṁśa pāribuṭi rakṣākari | 73 |
<P>subidhāna bacana ẏebe kaha pitāmaha
<P>yesaneke pāṇḍebaṁka tule kaurobaṁkara baḍhai seneha | 74 |
<P>yadyapi kāryya tumbhe kari nuāriba sanddha
<P>athabā pāṇḍabanta tiāra prabodhi | 75 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa bacane badaẏanti bhūrisarba
<P>ādihuṁ ẏemanta kathā na bhāḷilu abā | 76 |
<P>śateputra jāta tora hoile yetebeḷe
<P>bidura prathame driyodhanaku dilā tora koḷe | 77 |
<P>bidure boile tāta baḍāi bicakṣaṇa ẏe putragoṭi
<P>māne mānagobinda hoiba kaicchā jagajveṭhī | 78 |
<P>hāthe padma pāẏe padma ẏehāra hāde acchi
<P>aharniśi kandhu ẏehāra na chāḍiba lacchī | 79 |

<P1>68- yesaneka kuṛhoi chaṛāi chāgaḷa jība
<>tesaneka karṇṇaku hoicchi abasthā parābhaba |(ka, cha, ṛha, ga)
[MBO-06-62]
<P>kaṭire kaṭi mekhaḷe chaḍābanti jānu
<P>kiṁśuka puṣya prāẏe diśilā rādhebara tanu | 70 |
<P>āṇṭhu goḍa pāda taḷipāra kānti
<P>pādara āṅguṣṭhi sahite ye chaḍābanti nibhānti | 71 |
<P>śarīra bikāśai mandāra paṣya oḷi
<P>cakate karddana ye trimaṇḍa jāṇi gaḷi | 72 |
<P>dāneṇa karṇṇa ye kaicchā jagajjeṭhī
<P>satya alaṁghita se yāhāra nāmagoṭi | 73 |
<P>taḷahātha kariṇa ye pātile purandara
<P>upra hātha kari karṇṇa dilā ye bāsaba nija kara | 74 |
<P>abheda kapaca baja chauṁrī amr̥ta kuṇḍaḷa beni
<P>ẏe tininti karṇṇa dilā satyabākya gheni | 75 |
<P>idaṁ bākye karṇṇa indra pādeṇa pariṇāmi
<P>yathā triputi bhaji ẏebe bije karibā debasvāmī | 76 |
<P>bāsaba debatā se sumarile mātaḷiki
<P>puṣyaka bibāna gheni bije sahasrākṣa ra tahiṁki | 77 |
<P1>70|1 “kaṭire kaṭi mekhaḷe chaḍābanti jānu” pare cha, ṭa pothire pāṭha :–
<P1>puṇihiṁ asāṣṭama se rādhebara tanu |
<P1>dekhiṇa praśaṁsā ye karanti debagaṇe
<P1>boḷanti dhanya dhanya aṭu āho boṅgrakarṇṇe |
<P1>tohore se kari huai ẏesaneka bidhāna
<P1>nāhiṁ nāhiṁ na dekhilā ẏe tini bhmabana |
<P1>ẏete boli debe ye antarīkṣe thāi
<P1>karṇṇakaiṁ praśaṁsā karuchanti sarbe rahi |
<P1>karṇṇa boilā re bega bega akri kāḍha
<P1>karṇṇara citta ye heuacchi dr̥ḍha |
<P1>śuṇiṇa kumara ye uchuḍanti dehī
<P1>dehayāka ye sehu chaḍāiṇanei |
[MBO-06-63]
<P>āśiṣa kalyāṇa kale sahasrākṣa bedabākye
<P>sādhu sādhu karṇṇa boli staśaṁmanti trailokye | 78 |
<P>abheda kabaca bajachauṁrī amr̥ta beni kuṇḍaḷa
<P>puṣyeka rathe ẏehānta gheni bijekale ākhaṇḍaḷa | 79 |
<P>mane dharante pabanu bege caḷai yeuṁṇa ratha
<P>dāna bhārāẏe kari se basilā bhūmigata | 80 |
<P>mātaḷi mukha chāhiṁ bolai suranāhā
<P>yibā amara svargeye puṣyeka ratha bege bāhā | 81 |
<P>mātaḷi boilā deba śuṇimā jambu bhedī
<P>dāna bhārāẏe ratha ye ākāśaku na khedi | 82 |
<P>yeuṁṇa mahādāna ghenilu debasvāmī
<P>dāna bhārāẏe ratha tora basilāka bhūmi | 83 |
<P>śuṇiṇa āśrija ye hoile surarāja
<P>athabā siddha kemante hoiba mora kāryya | 84 |
<P>mātaḷi boilā ye atiẏa dānabhārā
<P>praigraha na dile ẏethi nāhiṁ pratikārā | 85 |
<P>svaranāthe boile puṣyeka rathe basi
<P>puṇa koḷeṇa karṇṇakaiṁ ye dhaile āśvāsi | 86 |
<P>indra debatāṁkara yahuṁ lāgilā karasthaḷi
<P>bāhuḍi karṇṇa dehe jaḍita roma baḷī | 87 |
<P>indra āśvāsanā kale yahuṁ karṇṇara kāẏe
<P>karṇṇara śarīra diśilā lohita barṇṇa prāẏe | 88 |
<P>hr̥de indra dile ye sahasa kigaṇa maṇi
<P>kaṇṇakaiṁ āśvāsanā kaleka bajramāṇi | 89 |
<P>bābu suputra śūrabanta sohaḍa bhāroi malla tu ye
<P>athabā amara svargakaiṁ muṁ kemante karibi bije | 90 |
<P1>89|2 karṇṇakaiṁ prārthanā kaleka bajapāṇi |(ña, ḍha, pha, ga, tha, ḍa, ba, ṅa)
<P1>90|1 bābu śūrabanta guṇabanta pucchai muhiṁ tote
<>akṣaẏa svargakaiṁ muṁ yibaiṁ kemante |
[MBO-06-64]
<P>karṇṇa boilā tumbhe yāasi pitāmaha
<P>āna kisa debaiṁ sandeśa mote kaha | 91 |
<P>indra boile muṁ dāna bhārā pāi
<P>br̥ndāarka meḷaku muṁ nuāribi yāi | 92 |
<P>tu yebe nandana mora mote śubha bāñcchuṁ
<P>ulaṭa pratigraha mote dāna māga kichu | 93 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā tāta ẏehā na miḷai yugata
<P>pitāuṁ putradāna ghenima kemanta | 94 |
<P>indra boilā putra mora pāra arthe
<P>tada nimante pratigraha dāna debaiṁ tote | 95 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā tāta muṁ māgibi yadyapi
<P>tu tāhā tāta dei nuāribu adyāpi | 96 |
<P>indra boile bābu ẏe mohora satya satya
<P>yāhā māgibu tāhā debaiṁ niẏata | 97 |
<P>taḷa hātha kariṇa magai bīra karṇṇa
<P>upara hāthare dāna diai maghabāna | 98 |
<P>śaṅkhu jaḷa tiḷa paḍante karṇṇa hāthe
<P>boilā amara svarga chāḍasi piṭa mote | 99 |
<P>śuṇiṇa thambībhūta ye hoile maghaba
<P>boile se amara bhmabana tote dei nuārai re bābā | 100 |
<P>tāhā chāḍiṇa āna māga ho sūryyabaḷā
<P>karṇṇa boilā tāta satyaku kalu heḷā | 101 |
<P>śuṇiṇa indra debatā karanteṇa sandeha
<P>karṇṇa boilā airābata gaja mote diasi pitāmaha | 102 |
<P>indra boile putra re ẏehā nuhai yugate
<P>se airābata gaja sādhya nuhai mote | 103 |
[MBO-06-65]
<P>hr̥dagate prameśi āna māgasi re bābu
<P>tu ye mohora putra mote mukati bāṭa debu | 104 |
<P>karṇṇa boile ho tāta nisate dāna dile
<P>dharma ki prāpata hoi sārthuka nohile | 105 |
<P>āna dāna mote yebe debu bajradhārī
<P>diasi pitā tohora rambhā apakṣarī | 106 |
<P>indra boile bābu se mohora baśya ye nohai
<P>rambhā nathile amara svarga na śohai | 107 |
<P>rambhākaiṁ chāḍi āna māgasi re bāḷa
<P>karṇṇa boilā tāta rahilu rabitaḷa | 108 |
<P>apāra prastābe tāra hoilu satyabhaṅga
<P>puṇa puṇa pāpabhārā heuacchi tora aṅga | 109 |
<P>tu mote prārthanā karipāribu ki debarāẏe
<P>śira kamaḷa kāṭi debaiṁ ẏehiṭhāẏe | 110 |
<P>indra boile tu dāneṇa śūrabantā
<P>satya tretaẏā dvāpara kaḷiyugare ruhāilu kathā | 111 |
<P>yuge yuge śūrabanta sarbadā badaẏanti ẏeṇe
<P>kapacadānī karṇṇa boli śubhilā baẏāṇe | 112 |
<P>karṇṇa boile tāta apāra kalu satyi
<P>diasi tāta mote bajra ye śakati | 113 |
<P>ẏehāuṁ tāta muṁ na māgai āna
<P>athabā diaki nadia bichāra maghabāna | 114 |
<P1>105|2 sārthuka = sātvika |
<P1>108 rambhāku chāḍiṇa āna māgasi re bābu
<>ẏebe nicaẏeṁ debiṭi yāhā bāñcchā karibu |(ja, da, ga)
<P1>112 yuga yuge śūrabanta rahi basu sarbakāḷe
<>kapacadānī karṇṇa boli śubhiba saẏaḷe |(ña, pha)
[MBO-06-66]
<P>idaṁbākya ye karṇṇara hoilā dr̥ṛhabāṇī
<P>suranātha āśrija hoilā tāhā śuṇi | 115 |
<P>mātaḷi boilā svāmī bhārā anu rūpe
<P>jāṇi parimāṇi tāta dāna debuna sarūpe | 116 |
<P>bāsaba debatā śuṇi tuṣṭa anumate
<P>bichārai bajra śakati muṁ debaiṁ kemante | 117 |
<P>bābu karṇṇa muṁ ye amare adhikārī
<P>daita dānaba mohora samaste bairi | 118 |
<P>airābrata piṭhire bajraśakati kare dekhi
<P>bhaẏeṇa durāntekamāne paḷānti samara upekṣi | 119 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā tāta kicchihiṁ deite nāhiṁ icchā
<P>ābara kete satyabhagna heu sahasrākṣā | 120 |
<P>mātaḷi boilā svāmī tu kaṣṭhora nakara hāde
<P>amara svargakaiṁ yibā karṇṇaku śahasra bege debe | 121 |
<P>indra sumaraṇā kale bajra ye śakati
<P>chaḍalakṣa yojanuṁ ye bikāśilā śahasrara jyoti | 122 |
<P>bajraśakati āsante kandare kale śaṁkā
<P>caturddaśa brahmāṇḍare lāgilā camakā | 123 |
<P>bhīṣmarūpa bikāśile deba surarāje
<P>mahā bajra śakati dhaileka bhmaje | 124 |
<P>śatedhārā śakati sahasre kiraṇa jyoti
<P>digāmbara puruṣamane dekhi mane kale bhīti | 125 |
<P>upara hātha kariṇa ye dileka maghabā
<P>karṇṇara hāthe dile surarāka debā | 126 |
<P>karṇṇara śarīra ye hoithilā kañchā
<P>śakati kariṇa lāgi hoilāka bajrasañchā | 127 |

[MBO-06-67]
<P>kapaca kuṇḍaḷa ye abheda bajra chauṁrī
<P>gheniṇa suranātha ye puṣyaka rathe bijekari | 128 |
<P>śakati chāḍante bāsaba hoilā nisteja
<P>karṇṇa boilā svāmī raha raha debarāja | 129 |
<P>svāmī mote śakati tu dilu satyabādī
<P>deba indra prāẏeka ye na diśilu jambhobhedī | 130 |
<P>yebe śakati nātha tu dilu satyabākye
<P>ẏe thāu tohora hāthe mohora udake | 131 |
<P>yetebeḷe mohore paḍai ẏethe kāryya
<P>māgile prasanne mote debu debarāja | 132 |
<P>indra śuṇi boile bābu ẏe apālaṭaka śara
<P>ẏehāra samāne deba asure karibu prahāra | 133 |
<P>ẏekai beḷeke ye se debaśasra peṣi
<P>digapāḷa hoile se abaśya āsibaṭi bināśi | 134 |
<P>karṇṇa boilā muṁ tāta māgibaiṁ yāhā
<P>sābadhāna hoi hāde śuṇimā deba tāhā | 135 |
<P>mahābhāratha yuddha muṁ śuṇiacchi karṇṇe
<P>samare māribi muhiṁ hari arajune | 136 |
<P>mātaḷi boilā deba kalu nice manda
<P>āpaṇā śahasre āpaṇāku hoilā pramāda | 137 |
<P1>129|2 “karṇṇa boilā svāmī raha raha debarāja” pare bahu pothire pāṭha :–
<P1>mohore śakati tu dilu ye saiti
<P1>deba indra prāẏe na diśilu surapati |

<P1>ẏe thāu tohora hāthe mohora diā ke |

<P1>137|2 āpaṇāra hāte putraku cintilu pramāde |(jha, ṭa, jha)
[MBO-06-68]
<P>indra boile mātaḷi tu mane na kara bhrānti
<P>karṇṇa ye boilā māribi hari arjuna duhinti | 138 |
<P>ẏekā arjunaku yebe māranti bolantā
<P>tebe se mora mane lāgantā hāde cintā | 139 |
<P>indra boile kr̥ṣṇa lāi śakati yebe karibaṭi bheda
<P>kadācite arjunaku na paḍiba pramāda | 140 |
<P>karṇṇakaiṁ sampāda ye bāsaba deba pucchi
<P>bābu trijībī hoithāa muṁ amare yāuacchi | 141 |

<P>nirbāta kapaca boli mūmralocana paṇanāti

[MBO-06-69]
<P>br̥ndāarka meḷe ye basilu amara svarge
<P>toṣe boili arjuna baramāga ẏebe bege | 149 |
<P>arjuna boilā mote yebe prasanna hoilu sahasrākṣa

<P>debataṁka thāi muṁ satyakali yāhā

[MBO-06-70]
<P>manuṣya hoiṇa se amara puraku śohai
<P>puṇa karṇṇa na thile ghāratha yuddha ye nohai | 161 |
<P>idaṁ bākya kahai ye amara svargabāsī
<P>bahuta purasari ye karṇṇakaiṁ praśaṁsi | 162 |
<P>bābu ẏeteka dāna mote dilāka sūryyabaḷā
<P>dāna bhārāre mora puṣyeka ratha na caḷilā | 163 |
<P>yahuṁ yāi nuārili muṁ amara bārasvatī
<P>pratigraha kari muṁ dili bajra ye śakati | 164 |
<P>boilā tu sākṣī hoithāa purandara
<P>ẏe śahasra gheni prahāra karibi śrīkr̥ṣṇa arjuna benibīra | 165 |
<P>indra boile śrīkr̥ṣṇa ẏe anibāraṇa śatedhārā śakati
<P>māgile karṇṇakaiṁ muṁ debiṭi ẏekaghānti | 166 |
<P>tāhā yebe bañchāi pāribuṭi bhārtha yuddhe
<P>pāṇḍabanta udita hoiba mahīmadhye | 167 |
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇāẏe boile parimāṇi bujha he śrībaccha
<P>ẏe śatadhārā śakatiki hāde ghaṭautkaṭa baḷibhakṣa | 168 |
<P>indra boile mā go tu yāhāra kuḷabadhū
<P>ubhaẏa kuḷa maṇḍaṇi mahimāṁ tora sādhu | 169 |
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇāẏe praṇapatya śrīkr̥ṣṇa pādapr̥ṣṭhe
<P>muhiṁ svargakaiṁ yāuacchi mote āgyāṁ debā he śrībatse | 170 |
<P>nārāẏaṇa padmapāda dhariṇa mahāsvatī
<P>nija prāṇa bisarjana hoilā tatakṣaṇānti | 171 |
<P>indra debatā śrīkr̥ṣṇāṁku puṣyeka rathare basāi
<P>amara bārasvatīki se bijaẏe surasāiṁ | 172 |
<P>sānanda menakā ye śakuntaḷāku dekhi
<P>pāilu nija bhmabana madhyabhmabana upekṣi | 173 |
[MBO-06-71]
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇāra mr̥tupiṇḍa gheni birāṭa mahātrodhī
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇa yujheṣṭhi ye birāṭakaiṁ prabodhi | 174 |
<P>mr̥tupiṇḍa dahana kari pretakāryya sāri
<P>benimāsa garbhabāsa hoilāni utturī | 175 |
<P>śaṅkha śveta uttara ye birāṭa putra tini

<P>bāruṇābante āsi rahile pañchujana | 178 |
<P>br̥ṣamāsa śukḷapakṣa tithi ye cauṭhī
<P>br̥haspatibāra punarbasu nakṣatra rukṣa ghaṭi | 179 |
<P>bāḷaba karaṇa śūḷa yogara prabeśa
<P>pāpayoga nāhiṁ lagna hoiacchi br̥ṣa | 180 |
<P>yātrā yoge yognī bāma beḷe

<P>yujheṣṭhiṁka agrateṇa pucchanti śrī puruṣottame
<P>muhiṁ dvārikāẏe yibi mote āgyām debā debadharme | 182 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile śuṇa jagannātha

<P>mohore sadaẏā ye na kale dhr̥tirāṣṭe

[MBO-06-72]
<P>nakuḷa kumāra guṇa tu jānu bāsudebe

<P>yujheṣṭhi debaṁkara bacane badaẏanti debahari

[MBO-06-134]
<P>āstāne basiacchi se rājā dhr̥tirāṣṭi

<P>rājāra śrabaṇe lāgi kahilā mantrī ye śakuni

[MBO-06-145]
<P>yadyapi ẏeka grāmakaiṁ debāra kariba

<P>śuṇa ho kurupati ẏehi nārāẏaṇa kathā

<P>āho driyodhana tu anīti kathā kahu

<P>driyodhana boilā yebe nirbāṇa hoiacchi

<P1>[pūrbapr̥ṣṭhāra pāṭhāntara] :–

<P>pimpuḍi bheḷā prāẏe lāgiṇa br̥kṣara

<P>kāhāra mukharu ye bāhāra rudhira

<P1>[pūrba pr̥ṣṭhāra pāṭhāntara] :–

<P>kāhāku diśilāka ulukāpāta prāẏe

<H>{@bhāradāra puboṅgjanma bibaraṇa@}
<P>ẏehā śuṇi pucchākale bilaṁka ādhipati
<P>bāḍāi sandeha kathā kahila agasti | 1 |
<P>bhāradā boliṇa ye boila madhyasvarge
<P>ẏeteka ucchaba indra kalāka kebaṇa bāge | 2 |

<P>śrīkāḷa jāṇai se bidyādhara svaẏeṁa | 6 |

<H>{@bīra hanumānaṅku āmantraṇa nimante
<>bhīmasenaṅkara gamana o apamāna@}
<P>bijaẏe dharmanandana indra praśasta āstāne
<P>yujheṣṭhideba pucchākale śrīpuruṣaṁka uttame | 1 |
<P>hari dhanabaḷe janabaḷe yehu baḷabantā
<P>keuṇasi guṇaku muṁ ye nohili śakatā | 2 |

<P>janeheṁ khinnata sarbeheṁ pañchubhrāthe | 3 |
<P>thāna ābori rahile dhr̥tirāṣṭaṁkara tanaẏe
<P>ābara kisa baḷabantā muhm bhīṣma droṇa karṇṇa bhūrisarba aśastamā kr̥paṁkara thaẏe | 4 |
<P>śakatā baḷabantā acchi ki moho yodhī

<P>śuṇiṇa mādhaba ye parama sānanda
<P>ẏekānte brikodaraku hakārile paramānanda | 6 |
<P1>1|2 “yujheṣṭhideba pucchākale śrīpuraṣaṁka uttame” pare
<>`ja, ta, ṭa, i, ka, da' pothire adhikā pāṭha :–
<P1>yujheṣṭhira bacane bolanti catradhara
<P1>maneṇa cintā tumbhe nakara nr̥pabara |
<P1>śatebhāi godhana sanya senā yete
<P1>mohora buddhibaḷe nāśayibe samaste |
<P1>bhīmasenaku hakāranti śrīhari
<P1>brikodaraku āśvāsi kahanti kaṁsa airi |
<P1>1|2 “yujheṣṭhi deba pucchākale śrīpuruṣaṁka uttame” pare
<>`ja, ta, ṭa, ṇa, ka, da' pothire adhikā pātha:–
<P1>hanumanta ṭhākuraṁku mora bahuta ārādhana
<P1>hanumanta ṭhāku mote peṣale janārddana |

<P>āpaṇe yogāḍile arghapātra gotiẏe
<P>tu yāa bhīmasena khinikhinā banasta yaẏe | 7 |
<P>hanumanta acchi se asknda nāme bana

<P>śuṇiṇa sānanda ye hoila pābeni

<P>āpaṇe śrīkr̥ṣṇa arjunara rathe sārathi

<P>hanumanta boilā re tahiṁki kimpe yibi

<P>ẏekāuna puruṣa pitr̥loke tāhāra hoanti svargagāmī | 122 |
<P>ẏe mohora pure yebe rahibu caturmāsyā
<P>taribe koṭiẏe puruṣa mohora ye āśā | 123 |
<P>mohora mukhe bolibi ki mora pure raha
<P>yāa bolibāku ta ye nohai muhiṁ raha | 124 |
<P>ẏe mahārāṣṭa chatriśa maṇḍaḷe muhiṁ ādhipati
<P>pr̥thī cintā karante mote dinata naaṇṭi | 125 |
<P>tumbaṁku kisa muṁ ye hoibi bhagati
<P>ẏe mohora mana ye cañjhaḷa prakr̥ti | 126 |
<P>raha boli boile bhagati hoi nuāribi
<P>yāa boli boile tora kopare nāśayibi | 127 |
<P>dr̥bhāsāẏe boile tu bhagati hoi nuāribu
<P>tohora kari jaṇeāmba sannidhyare deithiru | 128 |
<P>kontabhoja boile mohora dohitā goṭiẏe tāhāra nāma kontī

<P>tahiṁra sanniddhe dr̥bhāsā raṁcile parṇṇakuṭī

[MBO-06-366]
<P>bābu kontabhoja rājā ye aputrika hoithilā
